Corporate Helicopters has a fantastic relationship with Callaway Winery and everything was timed perfectly. Mr. Frost not only made us feel safe and like we were having fun, but it is obvious that he genuinely enjoys etching this joyous experience into people‚Äôs lives.

Fantastic!!!! I have gone on helicopter trips only 3 times in my lifetime (I am 53). At 17yrs from Las Vegas through the Grand Canyon with my parents, and then 2 years ago over Manhattan with my daughter.
Now, what this trip did not have the same in sights to offer, but it sure was compensated by the service and flight experience.  Very quaint, very friendly.  San Diego and its coast are beautiful.  The ground staff and the pilot just fantastic.  Unlike the "commercial" feeling of the other trips, this one is like going on a flight with your friend who is the pilot.

Corporate Helis is not rated 4.9 of 5 on google for no reason.  I shall come back to take their longer distance Mexico trips as well.
A grand experience! And I do travel the world!<//review>

<Pictures>None</Pictures><rating>5</rating>< Review>
WOW!!  What a wonderful experience with Corporate Helicopters.  I first learned about this company on FOX News when Heather, Fox Reporter, was interviewing one of Corporate Helicopter's Pilots, Peter.  It was a great interview and from this exposure I decided to go to their location and check it out.  Upon arriving I met Jesse, Flight Coordinator, who booked my Valentine Flight.  I was excited that I had an opportunity to pick and reserve a time on Valentine's Day since they are so popular they book up quickly.  Once we arrived we were met by Jesse, and Mandy, Operations Manager, who is so extremely nice and fun to talk to.  Mandy offered us some champagne and handed my wife some roses and then introduced us to Amanda, who gave us a tutorial on our flight.  Amanda then drove us out to the flight deck area via a golf cart and we boarded this very nice Helicopter which is made in Torrance California.  It is a beautiful Helicopter that sits four people counting the Pilot.  Our Pilot turned out to be Peter who was in the interview with Heather.  The flight was smooth quite and our Pilot, Peter, was superb.  We went from Montgomery Field to north of Mt. Soledad, north of Torrey Pines and looped back along the coast at about 1,000 feet.  As we went over the ocean we spotted a California Gray Whale, the water was so clear and the whale was right below us.  The flight hugged the coast line down to Mission Beach over Sea World, then south to San Diego Bay, down to the Coronado Bridge, circle around downtown and over Petco Park and back to Montgomery Field.  It was such a beautiful flight and Peter explained so many things throughout the flight that made the trip that much more interesting.  I highly recommend you take the time to check out Corporate Helicopters and you too will find yourself booking a flight that will leave you with sense of joy and satisfaction and a true thrill.  Very awesome!!!< /Review>

The shredded beef guisado style taco stands out here. The innovation of putting a ropa vieja into a taco is worth the trip if you're not from the area. <response>None< /response><Review>The veggie  burrito was flavorful</Review><user_id>104560200653777037675</user_id><time>1558443894568</time><pictures>None</pictures><name>Tanisha B</name></record></dataset><record>

106304859915860891916<//user>
<name>Jennifer Hunker<//name><date>1472836385399<//date><rate>5<//rate>< review>
The reviews are true.

WHAT IT IS
A little taco spot, tucked away sort of perpendicular to Spaghetti Eddie's.

WHAT YOU SHOULD ORDER
Tacos (especially the al pasteur and carne asada!)

AMBIANCE
N/A
I'm not deducting points for this, because this really is a takeout spot. Just be aware--this is NOT the sort of place where you can expect to sit down with a large party. There's maybe space for ten people in the entire store, it's that small. It's best to call ahead and order so you can pick up and jet outta there, because it gets crowded on Taco Tuesday.

FOOD AND DRINKS
5 Stars
These are probably the *best* tacos I've had anywhere. The meat is just so flavorful, and I haven't bumped into any nasty problems like tendons in the tacos. I usually get the al pasteur or carne asada, which is tender and delicious. Their nachos, sopes, and taquitos are amazing too!

NICE SURPRISES
TACO TUESDAY.

OVERALL
A real hidden gem for Glendora. This place is just incredible, and it's a shame it's in such a weird spot.< /review>

< Review>
I‚Äôve passed this place many times when going to the CostCo on Fenton Pkwy, but have never tried. My family had a craving for Japanese food and Sushi Kuchi is the closest and open for takeout.

A cute young lady named Min greeted me with enthusiasm and a smile. I can‚Äôt recall everything I ordered, but here‚Äôre the highlights. Soft shell crab, gyoza, calamari, and shrimp tempura for appetizers. Crispy fish, Hungry roll (I was hungry), Homeless roll (I try to support the homeless), Sensual Pleasure roll (I uhm... Never mind), White Boy roll (For my sisters white boyfriend). Honestly I‚Äôm not really a sushi person so I ordered the rolls based on their name.

In short, everything tasted fresh and delicious. There was a steady flow of customers while I waited for my food. Plenty of wasabi, ginger and I asked for low sodium soy sauce which they provided in plenty. I plan to return and highly recommend.< /Review>

I especially enjoyed the hungry roll which has popcorn lobster on top and the superman burrito.  Looking forward to trying more of their rolls!<//Text>
